  <activity role='ED clinician' action='estimate the impact of admission on life expectancy' objects='prognostic information, overall clinical status' id='activity15c'/>
  <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway05'>
    <branch condition='one or more high-risk markers present' id='branch28'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='document that one or more high-risk markers are present and proceed to specific marker documentation' objects='risk assessment summary' id='activity23a'/>
      <inclusiveGateway id='inclusiveGateway01'>
        <branch condition='respiratory distress present' id='branch13'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document respiratory distress as a high-risk marker' objects='respiratory assessment' id='activity16'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='hypoxemia present' id='branch14'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document hypoxemia as a high-risk marker' objects='oxygen saturation results' id='activity17'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='pulmonary edema is severe' id='branch15'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document severity of pulmonary edema as a high-risk marker' objects='clinical assessment, chest x-ray' id='activity18'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='poor response to diuresis documented' id='branch16'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document poor response to furosemide as a high-risk marker' objects='diuresis response assessment' id='activity19'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='hemodynamic compromise present' id='branch17'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document hemodynamic compromise as a high-risk marker' objects='hemodynamic assessment' id='activity20'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='significant arrhythmias present' id='branch18'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document significant arrhythmias as a high-risk marker' objects='electrocardiogram, rhythm assessment' id='activity21'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='troponin is positive' id='branch19'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document positive troponin as a high-risk marker' objects='troponin result' id='activity22'/>
        </branch>
      </inclusiveGateway>
    </branch>
    <branch condition='no high-risk markers identified' id='branch29'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='continue disposition planning without high-risk markers' objects='risk assessment summary' id='activity23'/>
    </branch>
  </exclusiveGateway>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='integrate EHMRG score, responsiveness to diuresis, high-risk markers, and overall clinical assessment to stratify patient intensity' objects='risk score, investigation results, clinical findings' id='activity24'/>
  <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway02'>
    <branch condition='requires noninvasive or invasive ventilation and/or intensive care unit care' id='branch21'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='classify patient as high intensity' objects='risk stratification result' id='activity25'/>
      <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway03'>
        <branch condition='higher level provider available at current hospital' id='branch22'>
          <activity role='critical care team' action='admit patient to intensive care unit with higher nurse-to-patient staffing and provide noninvasive or invasive ventilation as needed' objects='ICU bed, ventilation support' id='activity26'/>
          <activity role='critical care team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity26a'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='higher level provider not available at current hospital' id='branch23'>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='activate the transfer pathway and identify the receiving higher level provider' objects='transfer pathway, receiving provider information' id='activity27a'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='communicate clinical handoff and send patient records' objects='patient records, handoff information' id='activity27b'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='arrange patient transport to the receiving higher level provider' objects='transport arrangement' id='activity27c'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation during transfer preparation and transport' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation, transport monitor' id='activity27d'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='execute patient transfer and complete handoff to the receiving higher level provider' objects='patient transfer, handoff information' id='activity27e'/>
          <activity role='receiving critical care team' action='admit patient to intensive care unit or equivalent higher-acuity service with higher nurse-to-patient staffing and provide ventilation as needed' objects='ICU bed, ventilation support' id='activity28'/>
          <activity role='receiving critical care team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity28a'/>

    </branch>
    <branch condition='EHMRG quintile 1 or 2 and responded to initial treatment in the emergency department and no other considerations require admission and no ventilation or intensive care unit need' id='branch24'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='classify patient as low intensity' objects='risk stratification result' id='activity29'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='treat patient in the emergency department or outpatient setting' objects='treatment plan' id='activity30'/>
      <activity role='nursing staff' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized for discharge' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity30a'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='communicate discharge summary and follow-up needs to the primary care provider' objects='discharge summary, follow-up plan' id='activity31a'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='schedule the primary care follow-up visit within days of discharge' objects='follow-up appointment' id='activity31b'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='discharge patient home without inpatient admission' objects='discharge plan' id='activity30b'/>
    </branch>
    <branch condition='EHMRG quintile 3 to 5 or other considerations warrant admission and no ventilation or intensive care unit need' id='branch25'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='classify patient as average intensity' objects='risk stratification result' id='activity32'/>
      <activity role='inpatient team' action='admit patient to inpatient care with normal nurse-to-patient staffing' objects='hospital bed, admission orders' id='activity33'/>
      <activity role='inpatient team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity33a'/>
    </branch>
  </exclusiveGateway>
</process>
suggestion:
Problem: The low-intensity branch in the exclusive gateway with id='exclusiveGateway02' is logically incomplete. The condition of branch id='branch24' only checks low EHMRG risk, response to initial treatment, other considerations, and no ICU/ventilation need, but it does not exclude patients with documented high-risk markers from the earlier assessment (for example, positive troponin, hypoxemia, significant arrhythmia, or poor response to diuresis). This can incorrectly send a patient to discharge even though the process has already identified higher-risk clinical features.

Suggested modification: Revise the branch conditions in the exclusive gateway with id='exclusiveGateway02' so that high-risk markers are explicitly included in disposition logic. For example:
- change branch id='branch24' condition to:  
  `EHMRG quintile 1 or 2 and responded to initial treatment in the emergency department and no other considerations require admission and no high-risk markers identified and no ventilation or intensive care unit need`
- change branch id='branch25' condition to:  
  `EHMRG quintile 3 to 5 or other considerations warrant admission or one or more high-risk markers are present, and no ventilation or intensive care unit need`

Reason: The process already performs high-risk marker identification before disposition. If those findings are not carried into the final gateway condition, the gateway does not reflect the clinical recommendations for acute heart failure risk stratification, and the branch logic becomes unsafe and potentially contradictory.
You need to modify the process text according to the suggestions and output it.
Be careful not to change the format:

An activity is represented as follows:

The exclusive gateway is represented as follows:

    <activity role='' action='' objects='' id=''/>
  </branch>
</inclusiveGateway>
At the end of the process, please output '</process>'

There are a few requirements that should be noted when generating process text:
    1) role, action, objects and id in an activity represent the subject of the activity, the activity behavior, the items needed to perform in the activity and the activity id, respectively.
    2) There are at least two branches within the exclusive gateway and the parallel gateway.
    3) Activity, gateway, and branch id attributes must be unique.
    4) When the branch in the exclusive gateway has a condition, fill the condition into the condition attribute. When the branch unconditional within the exclusive gateway, the condition attribute of the branch =''. However, all branches within a exclusive gateway can only be conditional, or both unconditional.
    5) The branch in the parallel gateway has no condition attribute.
    6) Each branch in the inclusive gateway must have condition.
    7) There must be at least one activity inside the branch tag.
    8) The activity of a sequential relation need not be represented by a gateway, that is, there is no 'sequenceGateway' label.

<process>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='apply the standardized risk assessment and stratification process when the patient presents to the emergency department' objects='risk-stratification tool, patient presentation' id='activity03'/>
  <activity role='nursing staff' action='initiate frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity11'/>
  <parallelGateway id='parallelGateway01'>
    <branch id='branch01'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='obtain serum creatinine and electrolyte levels' objects='blood samples' id='activity04'/>
    </branch>
    <branch id='branch02'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='obtain troponin measurements' objects='blood samples' id='activity05'/>
    </branch>
    <branch id='branch03'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='obtain complete blood count' objects='blood samples' id='activity06'/>
    </branch>
    <branch id='branch04'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='perform electrocardiogram' objects='electrocardiogram' id='activity07'/>
    </branch>
    <branch id='branch05'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='perform chest x-ray examination' objects='chest x-ray' id='activity08'/>
    </branch>
    <branch id='branch06'>
      <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway01'>
        <branch condition='no recent echocardiogram available' id='branch07'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='perform echocardiogram' objects='echocardiogram' id='activity09'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='recent echocardiogram available' id='branch08'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='review recent echocardiogram result' objects='recent echocardiogram' id='activity10'/>
        </branch>
      </exclusiveGateway>
    </branch>
    <branch id='branch10'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='administer initial emergency department treatment including furosemide for diuresis' objects='furosemide, supportive therapy' id='activity12'/>
    </branch>
  </parallelGateway>
  <parallelGateway id='parallelGateway02'>
    <branch id='branch11'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='assess urine output, symptom relief, and hemodynamic response after furosemide' objects='diuresis response, clinical status' id='activity13a'/>
      <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway04'>
        <branch condition='adequate response to diuresis' id='branch26'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document adequate response to diuresis' objects='diuresis response assessment' id='activity13b'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='poor response to diuresis' id='branch27'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document poor response to diuresis' objects='diuresis response assessment' id='activity13c'/>
        </branch>
      </exclusiveGateway>
    </branch>
    <branch id='branch12'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='collect required clinical variables and investigation results for EHMRG calculation' objects='clinical data, investigation results' id='activity14a'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='calculate EHMRG score and assign risk quintile' objects='clinical data, investigation results, EHMRG tool' id='activity14b'/>
    </branch>
  </parallelGateway>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='review advanced directives and goals of care' objects='advanced directives, goals of care information' id='activity15a'/>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='assess cognitive status including severe dementia' objects='cognitive status, collateral history' id='activity15b'/>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='estimate the impact of admission on life expectancy' objects='prognostic information, overall clinical status' id='activity15c'/>
  <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway05'>
    <branch condition='one or more high-risk markers present' id='branch28'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='document that one or more high-risk markers are present and proceed to specific marker documentation' objects='risk assessment summary' id='activity23a'/>
      <inclusiveGateway id='inclusiveGateway01'>
        <branch condition='respiratory distress present' id='branch13'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document respiratory distress as a high-risk marker' objects='respiratory assessment' id='activity16'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='hypoxemia present' id='branch14'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document hypoxemia as a high-risk marker' objects='oxygen saturation results' id='activity17'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='pulmonary edema is severe' id='branch15'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document severity of pulmonary edema as a high-risk marker' objects='clinical assessment, chest x-ray' id='activity18'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='poor response to diuresis documented' id='branch16'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document poor response to furosemide as a high-risk marker' objects='diuresis response assessment' id='activity19'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='hemodynamic compromise present' id='branch17'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document hemodynamic compromise as a high-risk marker' objects='hemodynamic assessment' id='activity20'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='significant arrhythmias present' id='branch18'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document significant arrhythmias as a high-risk marker' objects='electrocardiogram, rhythm assessment' id='activity21'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='troponin is positive' id='branch19'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document positive troponin as a high-risk marker' objects='troponin result' id='activity22'/>
        </branch>
      </inclusiveGateway>
    </branch>
    <branch condition='no high-risk markers identified' id='branch29'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='continue disposition planning without high-risk markers' objects='risk assessment summary' id='activity23'/>
    </branch>
  </exclusiveGateway>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='integrate EHMRG score, responsiveness to diuresis, high-risk markers, and overall clinical assessment to stratify patient intensity' objects='risk score, investigation results, clinical findings' id='activity24'/>
  <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway02'>
    <branch condition='requires noninvasive or invasive ventilation and/or intensive care unit care' id='branch21'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='classify patient as high intensity' objects='risk stratification result' id='activity25'/>
      <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway03'>
        <branch condition='higher level provider available at current hospital' id='branch22'>
          <activity role='critical care team' action='admit patient to intensive care unit with higher nurse-to-patient staffing and provide noninvasive or invasive ventilation as needed' objects='ICU bed, ventilation support' id='activity26'/>
          <activity role='critical care team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity26a'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='higher level provider not available at current hospital' id='branch23'>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='activate the transfer pathway and identify the receiving higher level provider' objects='transfer pathway, receiving provider information' id='activity27a'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='communicate clinical handoff and send patient records' objects='patient records, handoff information' id='activity27b'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='arrange patient transport to the receiving higher level provider' objects='transport arrangement' id='activity27c'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation during transfer preparation and transport' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation, transport monitor' id='activity27d'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='execute patient transfer and complete handoff to the receiving higher level provider' objects='patient transfer, handoff information' id='activity27e'/>
          <activity role='receiving critical care team' action='admit patient to intensive care unit or equivalent higher-acuity service with higher nurse-to-patient staffing and provide ventilation as needed' objects='ICU bed, ventilation support' id='activity28'/>
          <activity role='receiving critical care team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity28a'/>
        </branch>
      </exclusiveGateway>
    </branch>
    <branch condition='EHMRG quintile 1 or 2 and responded to initial treatment in the emergency department and no other considerations require admission and no high-risk markers identified and no ventilation or intensive care unit need' id='branch24'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='classify patient as low intensity' objects='risk stratification result' id='activity29'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='treat patient in the emergency department or outpatient setting' objects='treatment plan' id='activity30'/>
      <activity role='nursing staff' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized for discharge' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity30a'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='communicate discharge summary and follow-up needs to the primary care provider' objects='discharge summary, follow-up plan' id='activity31a'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='schedule the primary care follow-up visit within days of discharge' objects='follow-up appointment' id='activity31b'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='discharge patient home without inpatient admission' objects='discharge plan' id='activity30b'/>
    </branch>
    <branch condition='EHMRG quintile 3 to 5 or other considerations warrant admission or one or more high-risk markers are present and no ventilation or intensive care unit need' id='branch25'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='classify patient as average intensity' objects='risk stratification result' id='activity32'/>
      <activity role='inpatient team' action='admit patient to inpatient care with normal nurse-to-patient staffing' objects='hospital bed, admission orders' id='activity33'/>
      <activity role='inpatient team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity33a'/>
    </branch>
  </exclusiveGateway>
</process>

| **task_prompt** | Episode of Care for Acute Heart Failure The Acute Heart Failure Episode-of-Care Advisory Panel developed the episode-of-care model for acute heart failure (Figure 6). Modules 1 through 3 represent the acute heart failure episode of care. The following recommendations include the recommendations from the clinical handbook on acute heart failure published in 2013 and updates to the recommendations (as noted in the What’s New box above). Figure 6. Episode-of-Care Model for Acute Heart Failure Module 1: Risk Stratification Module 1 Recommended Practices 1.1 Risk Assessment/Stratification Risk-stratification tools that can be used for multiple conditions (including HF) should be developed and consistently applied across all Ontario hospitals. 1.2 Responsiveness to Diuresis Initial investigations should include: • serum creatinine and electrolyte levels • troponin measurements • complete blood count • electrocardiogram • chest x-ray examination • an echocardiogram if no recent echocardiogram is available • frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until patient is stabilized 1.3 Risk Stratification Patient Groups Low intensity: Patients can be treated in the ED or in outpatient settings and discharged home without requiring inpatient admission. However, these patients require a follow-up visit with their primary care provider within days of discharge from the ED. Average intensity: Patients require admission to inpatient care with normal nurse-to-patient staffing. High intensity: Patients require ventilation (either noninvasive or invasive ventilation) and/or admission to an intensive care unit with higher nurse-to-patient staffing. High-risk markers include: • respiratory distress • hypoxemia • severity of pulmonary edema • poor response to furosemide administered in ED • hemodynamic compromise • significant arrhythmias • positive troponin 1.4 Heart Failure Risk Score An acute heart failure risk score—for example, the EHMRG—be calculated to assist with clinical decision-making and predicting the 7-day mortality risk of HF patients (predicted mortality risk increases incrementally with higher EHMRG risk score). As a general guide, patients who are low-risk (e.g., EHMRG quintiles 1 and 2) can be considered for discharge home if they have responded to initial treatment in the ED, provided that there are no other considerations (e.g., advanced-directives, severe dementia, estimated impact of admission on life-expectancy, etc.). Patients who are at higher-risk (e.g., EHMRG quintiles 3-5) should be admitted to hospital. Abbreviations: ACCF, American College of Cardiology Foundation; AHA, American Heart Association; CCS, Canadian Cardiovascular Society; ED, emergency department; EHMRG, Emergency Heart Failure Mortality Risk Grade; HF, heart failure; NICE, National Institute for Clinical Excellence. Module 1 Implementation Considerations General Considerations for Risk Stratification • Hospitals should use a common standardized risk stratification assessment tool or process to determine where and how to assist with clinical decision making when patients present to the emergency department. • All hospitals should have a pathway or mechanism to transfer patients to a higher level provider |

[You're a process design reviewer. Now, we share a common interest in collaborating to successfully complete a task assigned by a new customer.
You are familiar with exclusive gateway, parallel gateway and inclusive gateway in BPMN. Your main responsibilities include give suggestion to the process.
Here is a new customer's task: Episode of Care for Acute Heart Failure

The Acute Heart Failure Episode-of-Care Advisory Panel developed the episode-of-care model for acute heart failure (Figure 6). Modules 1 through 3 represent the acute heart failure episode of care. The following recommendations include the recommendations from the clinical handbook on acute heart failure published in 2013 and updates to the recommendations (as noted in the What’s New box above).

Figure 6. Episode-of-Care Model for Acute Heart Failure

Module 1: Risk Stratification

Module 1 Recommended Practices

1.1 Risk Assessment/Stratification
Risk-stratification tools that can be used for multiple conditions (including HF) should be developed and consistently applied across all Ontario hospitals.

1.2 Responsiveness to Diuresis
Initial investigations should include:
• serum creatinine and electrolyte levels
• troponin measurements
• complete blood count
• electrocardiogram
• chest x-ray examination
• an echocardiogram if no recent echocardiogram is available
• frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until patient is stabilized

1.3 Risk Stratification Patient Groups
Low intensity: Patients can be treated in the ED or in outpatient settings and discharged home without requiring inpatient admission. However, these patients require a follow-up visit with their primary care provider within days of discharge from the ED.
Average intensity: Patients require admission to inpatient care with normal nurse-to-patient staffing.
High intensity: Patients require ventilation (either noninvasive or invasive ventilation) and/or admission to an intensive care unit with higher nurse-to-patient staffing.

High-risk markers include:
• respiratory distress
• hypoxemia
• severity of pulmonary edema
• poor response to furosemide administered in ED
• hemodynamic compromise
• significant arrhythmias
• positive troponin

1.4 Heart Failure Risk Score
An acute heart failure risk score—for example, the EHMRG—be calculated to assist with clinical decision-making and predicting the 7-day mortality risk of HF patients (predicted mortality risk increases incrementally with higher EHMRG risk score).

As a general guide, patients who are low-risk (e.g., EHMRG quintiles 1 and 2) can be considered for discharge home if they have responded to initial treatment in the ED, provided that there are no other considerations (e.g., advanced-directives, severe dementia, estimated impact of admission on life-expectancy, etc.). Patients who are at higher-risk (e.g., EHMRG quintiles 3-5) should be admitted to hospital.

Abbreviations: ACCF, American College of Cardiology Foundation; AHA, American Heart Association; CCS, Canadian Cardiovascular Society; ED, emergency department; EHMRG, Emergency Heart Failure Mortality Risk Grade; HF, heart failure; NICE, National Institute for Clinical Excellence.

Module 1 Implementation Considerations
General Considerations for Risk Stratification
• Hospitals should use a common standardized risk stratification assessment tool or process to determine where and how to assist with clinical decision making when patients present to the emergency department.
• All hospitals should have a pathway or mechanism to transfer patients to a higher level provider.
To complete the task, I will give you one or more instructions, and you must help me to write a specific solution that appropriately solves the requested instruction based on your expertise and my needs.]

        <branch condition='recent echocardiogram available' id='branch08'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='review recent echocardiogram result' objects='recent echocardiogram' id='activity10'/>
        </branch>
      </exclusiveGateway>
    </branch>
    <branch id='branch10'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='administer initial emergency department treatment including furosemide for diuresis' objects='furosemide, supportive therapy' id='activity12'/>
    </branch>
  </parallelGateway>
  <parallelGateway id='parallelGateway02'>
    <branch id='branch11'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='assess urine output, symptom relief, and hemodynamic response after furosemide' objects='diuresis response, clinical status' id='activity13a'/>
      <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway04'>
        <branch condition='adequate response to diuresis' id='branch26'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document adequate response to diuresis' objects='diuresis response assessment' id='activity13b'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='poor response to diuresis' id='branch27'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document poor response to diuresis' objects='diuresis response assessment' id='activity13c'/>
        </branch>
      </exclusiveGateway>
    </branch>
    <branch id='branch12'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='collect required clinical variables and investigation results for EHMRG calculation' objects='clinical data, investigation results' id='activity14a'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='calculate EHMRG score and assign risk quintile' objects='clinical data, investigation results, EHMRG tool' id='activity14b'/>
    </branch>
  </parallelGateway>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='review advanced directives and goals of care' objects='advanced directives, goals of care information' id='activity15a'/>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='assess cognitive status including severe dementia' objects='cognitive status, collateral history' id='activity15b'/>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='estimate the impact of admission on life expectancy' objects='prognostic information, overall clinical status' id='activity15c'/>
  <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway05'>
    <branch condition='one or more high-risk markers present' id='branch28'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='document that one or more high-risk markers are present and proceed to specific marker documentation' objects='risk assessment summary' id='activity23a'/>
      <inclusiveGateway id='inclusiveGateway01'>
        <branch condition='respiratory distress present' id='branch13'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document respiratory distress as a high-risk marker' objects='respiratory assessment' id='activity16'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='hypoxemia present' id='branch14'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document hypoxemia as a high-risk marker' objects='oxygen saturation results' id='activity17'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='pulmonary edema is severe' id='branch15'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document severity of pulmonary edema as a high-risk marker' objects='clinical assessment, chest x-ray' id='activity18'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='poor response to diuresis documented' id='branch16'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document poor response to furosemide as a high-risk marker' objects='diuresis response assessment' id='activity19'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='hemodynamic compromise present' id='branch17'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document hemodynamic compromise as a high-risk marker' objects='hemodynamic assessment' id='activity20'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='significant arrhythmias present' id='branch18'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document significant arrhythmias as a high-risk marker' objects='electrocardiogram, rhythm assessment' id='activity21'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='troponin is positive' id='branch19'>
          <activity role='ED clinician' action='document positive troponin as a high-risk marker' objects='troponin result' id='activity22'/>
        </branch>
      </inclusiveGateway>
    </branch>
    <branch condition='no high-risk markers identified' id='branch29'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='continue disposition planning without high-risk markers' objects='risk assessment summary' id='activity23'/>
    </branch>
  </exclusiveGateway>
  <activity role='ED clinician' action='integrate EHMRG score, responsiveness to diuresis, high-risk markers, and overall clinical assessment to stratify patient intensity' objects='risk score, investigation results, clinical findings' id='activity24'/>
  <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway02'>
    <branch condition='requires noninvasive or invasive ventilation and/or intensive care unit care' id='branch21'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='classify patient as high intensity' objects='risk stratification result' id='activity25'/>
      <exclusiveGateway id='exclusiveGateway03'>
        <branch condition='higher level provider available at current hospital' id='branch22'>
          <activity role='critical care team' action='admit patient to intensive care unit with higher nurse-to-patient staffing and provide noninvasive or invasive ventilation as needed' objects='ICU bed, ventilation support' id='activity26'/>
          <activity role='critical care team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity26a'/>
        </branch>
        <branch condition='higher level provider not available at current hospital' id='branch23'>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='activate the transfer pathway and identify the receiving higher level provider' objects='transfer pathway, receiving provider information' id='activity27a'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='communicate clinical handoff and send patient records' objects='patient records, handoff information' id='activity27b'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='arrange patient transport to the receiving higher level provider' objects='transport arrangement' id='activity27c'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation during transfer preparation and transport' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation, transport monitor' id='activity27d'/>
          <activity role='hospital transfer team' action='execute patient transfer and complete handoff to the receiving higher level provider' objects='patient transfer, handoff information' id='activity27e'/>
          <activity role='receiving critical care team' action='admit patient to intensive care unit or equivalent higher-acuity service with higher nurse-to-patient staffing and provide ventilation as needed' objects='ICU bed, ventilation support' id='activity28'/>
          <activity role='receiving critical care team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity28a'/>
        </branch>
      </exclusiveGateway>
    </branch>
    <branch condition='EHMRG quintile 1 or 2 and responded to initial treatment in the emergency department and no other considerations require admission and no high-risk markers identified and no ventilation or intensive care unit need' id='branch24'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='classify patient as low intensity' objects='risk stratification result' id='activity29'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='treat patient in the emergency department or outpatient setting' objects='treatment plan' id='activity30'/>
      <activity role='nursing staff' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized for discharge' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity30a'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='communicate discharge summary and follow-up needs to the primary care provider' objects='discharge summary, follow-up plan' id='activity31a'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='schedule the primary care follow-up visit within days of discharge' objects='follow-up appointment' id='activity31b'/>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='discharge patient home without inpatient admission' objects='discharge plan' id='activity30b'/>
    </branch>
    <branch condition='EHMRG quintile 3 to 5 or other considerations warrant admission or one or more high-risk markers are present and no ventilation or intensive care unit need' id='branch25'>
      <activity role='ED clinician' action='classify patient as average intensity' objects='risk stratification result' id='activity32'/>
      <activity role='inpatient team' action='admit patient to inpatient care with normal nurse-to-patient staffing' objects='hospital bed, admission orders' id='activity33'/>
      <activity role='inpatient team' action='continue frequent measurement of heart rate, blood pressure, and oxygen saturation until the patient is stabilized' objects='vital signs, oxygen saturation' id='activity33a'/>
    </branch>
  </exclusiveGateway>
